# Security Information

## Device
### Software Versions
	- Installed version:	V4.66 Release
	- Newest version:		V4.70.05 Beta


### Security Level and Communication Services
	- Security level:	0
	- recommended security level:	4

| Name                 | State       | Secure |
|----------------------|-------------|--------|
| Telnet               | activated   | NO     |
| FTP Server           | activated   | NO     |
| NFS Server           | deactivated | YES    |
| Console Interface    | activated   | NO     |
| SNMP                 | deactivated | YES    |
| SMI Connection Limit | not limited | NO     |
